This project (code-named **‚ÄúMediaProcessor‚Äù**) automatically **splits long recordings**, transcribes speech to text using **OpenAI Whisper**, and then analyzes the transcripts with **GPT-4** to extract insights. The pipeline was developed to turn hours of media (podcasts, videos, songs) into structured data and summaries without manual effort. It includes a **context-preserving splitter** (‚ÄúOuroboros Splitter‚Äù) that uses FFmpeg to chunk media while keeping context, a **Whisper transcription engine**, and a **GPT-based analyzer** that derives keywords, themes, or metadata (nicknamed ‚ÄúChaosMerger‚Äù when compiling results into CSV or JSON). The output can be a neatly formatted transcript, a summary analysis (e.g. sentiments, themes, or even creative cues), and combined datasets for further use. This tool exemplifies ‚Äú**AI Alchemy**‚Äù ‚Äì transforming raw audiovisual chaos into organized creative gold.\n\n**Tags:** Python, OpenAI Whisper, GPT-4, FFmpeg, Automation, Data Pipeline\n\n```python\n# Snippet: Transcription & Analysis with Whisper + GPT-3.5/4\nwith open(audio_path, \"rb\") as audio:\n    transcript = openai_client.audio.transcribe(\"whisper-1\", audio).text\n# ... (save transcript) ...\nresponse = openai_client.chat.completions.create(\n    model=\"gpt-3.5-turbo\",\n    messages=[{\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"Analyze the transcript for themes...\"}, \n              {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": transcript}],\n    max_tokens=300, temperature=0.7\n)\nanalysis = response.choices[0].message.content.strip()\n```\n\n### **Auto-YouTube**  \n\n**Description:** An **automated YouTube video creator** that generates full-length videos (and Shorts) from real-time content (e.g. news feeds) with zero manual editing. This means the user orchestrated a multi-layer automation: Python -> AppleScript -> Photoshop JavaScript, to achieve what normally would require tedious manual work or expensive plugin. (open each image file, resize and position it into the grid) ...\n\"\"\"\napple_script = f'''\ntell application \"Adobe Photoshop 2021\"\n    activate\n    do javascript \"{js_code}\"\nend tell\n'''\nrun_applescript(apple_script)  # Executes the automation in Photoshop\n```\n\n### **Photoshop Mockup Automation**  \n\n**Description:** This project targets the automation of **mockup creation** in Photoshop.             "content": "import os\nimport time\nfrom datetime import datetime\n\nfrom PIL import Image, UnidentifiedImageError\nfrom tqdm import tqdm\n\n# Constants\nMAX_WIDTH, MAX_HEIGHT = 2250, 2700\nTARGET_DPI = 300\nBATCH_SIZE = 50\nPAUSE_DURATION = 5\nMIN_FILE_SIZE_BYTES = 8 * 1024 * 1024  # 8MB in bytes\n\n# Aspect Ratio Minimums\nASPECT_RATIO_MINIMUMS = {\n    \"16:9\": (720, 1280),  # Landscape\n    \"9:16\": (1080, 1920),  # Portrait\n    \"1:1\": (1024, 1024),  # Square\n}\n\n\n# Function to get the closest aspect ratio\ndef get_closest_aspect_ratio(width, height):\n    aspect_ratios = {\n        \"16:9\": 16 / 9,\n        \"9:16\": 9 / 16,\n        \"1:1\": 1 / 1,\n    }\n    current_ratio = width / height\n    closest_ratio = min(\n        aspect_ratios, key=lambda ar: abs(current_ratio - aspect_ratios[ar])\n    )\n    return closest_ratio, ASPECT_RATIO_MINIMUMS[closest_ratio]\n\n\n# Function to apply 300 DPI to an image\ndef apply_dpi(im, output_path):\n    im.save(output_path, dpi=(300, 300), quality=85)\n    print(f\"‚úÖ Applied 300 DPI to: {output_path}\")\n\n\n# Function to resize images\ndef resize_image(im, output_path):\n    width, height = im.size\n    closest_ratio, (min_width, min_height) = get_closest_aspect_ratio(width, height)\n    aspect_ratio = width / height\n\n    # Determine new dimensions\n    if width < min_width or height < min_height:\n        if closest_ratio == \"16:9\":\n            new_width, new_height = min_width, int(min_width / aspect_ratio)\n        elif closest_ratio == \"9:16\":\n            new_height, new_width = min_height, int(min_height * aspect_ratio)\n        elif closest_ratio == \"1:1\":\n            new_width, new_height = max(min_width, min_height), max(\n                min_width, min_height\n            )\n    elif width > MAX_WIDTH or height > MAX_HEIGHT:\n        if width / MAX_WIDTH > height / MAX_HEIGHT:\n            new_width, new_height = MAX_WIDTH, int(MAX_WIDTH / aspect_ratio)\n        else:\n            new_height, new_width = MAX_HEIGHT, int(MAX_HEIGHT * aspect_ratio)\n    else:\n        new_width, new_height = width, height\n\n    print(f\"üîÑ Resizing to: {new_width}x{new_height}\")\n    im = im.resize((new_width, new_height), Image.LANCZOS)\n    im.save(output_path, dpi=(TARGET_DPI, TARGET_DPI), quality=85)\n\n\n# Function to process a batch of images\ndef process_batch(batch, root):\n    for file in tqdm(batch, desc=\"üîÑ Processing batch\"):\n        file_path = os.path.join(root, file)\n        file_ext = file.lower().split(\".\")[-1]\n\n        # Skip unsupported file formats\n        if file_ext not in (\"jpg\", \"jpeg\", \"png\"):\n            print(f\"‚ö†Ô∏è Skipping {file}: Unsupported file format.\")\n            continue\n\n        try:\n            im = Image.open(file_path)\n            width, height = im.size\n            print(f\"\\nüñºÔ∏è Processing {file}: Original size: {width}x{height}\")\n\n            # Apply DPI\n            temp_file_dpi = os.path.join(root, f\"300dpi_{file}\")\n            apply_dpi(im, temp_file_dpi)\n\n            # Resize the image\n            temp_file_resize = os.path.join(root, f\"resized_{file}\")\n            resize_image(Image.open(temp_file_dpi), temp_file_resize)\n\n            # Replace the original file with the resized image\n            os.rename(temp_file_resize, file_path)\n            os.remove(temp_file_dpi)  # Clean up intermediate DPI-adjusted file\n\n            print(f\"‚úÖ Successfully resized {file} with 300 DPI\")\n\n        except UnidentifiedImageError:\n            print(f\"‚ö†Ô∏è Skipping {file}: Cannot identify image.\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"‚ö†Ô∏è Error processing {file}: {e}\")\n\n\n# Process images\ndef process_images(source_directory):\n    batch = []\n    for root, _, files in os.walk(source_directory):\n        for file in files:\n            batch.append(file)\n            if len(batch) >= BATCH_SIZE:\n                process_batch(batch, root)\n                batch = []\n                print(f\"‚è∏Ô∏è Pausing for {PAUSE_DURATION} seconds...\")\n                time.sleep(PAUSE_DURATION)\n\n        if batch:\n            process_batch(batch, root)\n            batch = []\n\n\n# Main function\ndef main():\n    source_directory = input(\n        \"Enter the path to the source directory containing images: \"\n    ).strip()\n    if not os.path.isdir(source_directory):\n        print(\"Source directory does not exist.\")\n        return\n\n    process_images(source_directory)\n    print(\"üéâ All images processed successfully!\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()"

            "content": "import os\nimport csv\nimport sys\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\nfrom termcolor import colored\nfrom openai import OpenAI\n\n# Load environment variables from .env file\nload_dotenv(dotenv_path=\"/Users/steven/.env\")\n\n# Get API key and validate it\napi_key = os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\")\nif not api_key:\n    raise EnvironmentError(\"‚ùå OpenAI API key not found. Please check your .env file.\")\n\n# Initialize OpenAI client\nclient = OpenAI(api_key=api_key)\n\n\n# Helper function to format timestamps\ndef format_timestamp(seconds):\n    \"\"\"Convert seconds into MM:SS format.\"\"\"\n    minutes = int(seconds // 60)\n    seconds = int(seconds % 60)\n    return f\"{minutes:02d}:{seconds:02d}\"\n\n\n# Function to transcribe audio using OpenAI's Whisper\ndef transcribe_audio(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Transcribe an audio file using OpenAI's Whisper API.\"\"\"\n    with open(file_path, \"rb\") as audio_file:\n        transcript_data = client.audio.transcribe(model=\"whisper-1\", file=audio_file, response_format=\"verbose_json\")\n\n    # Process transcript with timestamps\n    transcript_with_timestamps = []\n    for segment in transcript_data.segments:\n        start_time = segment[\"start\"]\n        end_time = segment[\"end\"]\n        text = segment[\"text\"]\n        transcript_with_timestamps.append(\n            f\"{format_timestamp(start_time)} -- {format_timestamp(end_time)}: {text}\"\n        )\n\n    return \"\\n\".join(transcript_with_timestamps)\n\n\n# Function to analyze multimedia content using GPT-4o\ndef analyze_text_for_section(transcript, section_number=1):\n    try:\n        response = client.chat.completions.create(model=\"gpt-4o\",  # Upgraded to GPT-4o\n        messages=[\n            {\n                \"role\": \"system\",\n                \"content\": (\n                    \"You are an expert multimedia analyst and storyteller. Create a folder for the song\n    os.makedirs(song_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n    # Step 1: Transcribe the audio file\n    print(f\"üéº Transcribing {file_name}...\")\n    transcript = transcribe_audio(file_path)\n    transcript_path = os.path.join(song_dir, f\"{file_name_no_ext}_transcript.txt\")\n    with open(transcript_path, \"w\") as f:\n        f.write(transcript)\n    print(f\"‚úÖ Transcript saved: {transcript_path}\")\n\n    #             "content": "import os\nimport shutil\nimport hashlib\n\n# Define the base directory\nbase_dir = \"/Users/steven/Music/nocTurneMeLoDieS/mp4\"\n\ndef hash_file(file_path):\n    \"\"\"Generate a hash for a file to identify duplicates.\"\"\"\n    hasher = hashlib.md5()\n    with open(file_path, 'rb') as f:\n        while chunk := f.read(8192):\n            hasher.update(chunk)\n    return hasher.hexdigest()\n\ndef flatten_directory(directory):\n    \"\"\"Move all files from nested folders to the base directory.\"\"\"\n    for root, _, files in os.walk(directory, topdown=False):\n        for file in files:\n            file_path = os.path.join(root, file)\n            destination_path = os.path.join(directory, file)\n\n            # Avoid overwriting files with the same name\n            if os.path.exists(destination_path):\n                base_name, ext = os.path.splitext(file)\n                counter = 1\n                while os.path.exists(destination_path):\n                    destination_path = os.path.join(directory, f\"{base_name}_{counter}{ext}\")\n                    counter += 1\n            \n            shutil.move(file_path, destination_path)\n            print(f\"Moved: {file_path} -> {destination_path}\")\n\n        # Remove empty folders\n        if not os.listdir(root):\n            os.rmdir(root)\n            print(f\"Removed empty folder: {root}\")\n\ndef remove_duplicates(directory):\n    \"\"\"Remove duplicate files based on their content.\"\"\"\n    seen_hashes = {}\n    for root, _, files in os.walk(directory):\n        for file in files:\n            file_path = os.path.join(root, file)\n            file_hash = hash_file(file_path)\n\n            if file_hash in seen_hashes:\n                print(f\"Duplicate found: {file_path} (same as {seen_hashes[file_hash]})\")\n                os.remove(file_path)\n                print(f\"Removed duplicate: {file_path}\")\n            else:\n                seen_hashes[file_hash] = file_path\n\ndef organize_by_type(directory):\n    \"\"\"Organize files into subfolders based on their type.\"\"\"\n    type_folders = {\n        \".mp3\": \"MP3s\",\n        \".txt\": \"Transcripts\",\n        \"_analysis.txt\": \"Analyses\"\n    }\n\n    for file in os.listdir(directory):\n        file_path = os.path.join(directory, file)\n\n        # Skip directories\n        if os.path.isdir(file_path):\n            continue\n\n        # Determine the folder based on the file extension or name pattern\n        destination_folder = None\n        for key, folder_name in type_folders.items():\n            if key in file:\n                destination_folder = folder_name\n                break\n\n        if not destination_folder:\n            destination_folder = \"Others\"\n\n        # Create the destination folder if it doesn't exist\n        destination_folder_path = os.path.join(directory, destination_folder)\n        os.makedirs(destination_folder_path, exist_ok=True)\n\n        # Move the file to the appropriate folder\n        shutil.move(file_path, os.path.join(destination_folder_path, file))\n        print(f\"Moved: {file} -> {destination_folder}/{file}\")\n\ndef clean_directory(directory):\n    \"\"\"Clean up the directory by flattening, removing duplicates, and organizing.\"\"\"\n    print(\"Flattening directory...\")\n    flatten_directory(directory)\n\n    print(\"Removing duplicate files...\")\n    remove_duplicates(directory)\n\n    print(\"Organizing files by type...\")\n    organize_by_type(directory)\n\n    print(\"‚úÖ Directory cleanup complete!\")\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    clean_directory(base_dir)"
